 2.022 SELECT  * WHERE   { ?name  <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label>  "Adam Nathanson"@en ;            <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/profession>  ?propertyval .   }
 134.879 PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> SELECT * WHERE { ?city a <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/Place>; rdfs:label 'Sinop'@en.  ?airport a <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/Airport>. {?airport <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/city> ?city} UNION {?airport <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/location> ?city} UNION {?airport <http://dbpedia.org/property/cityServed> ?city.} UNION {?airport <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/city> ?city. }{?airport <http://dbpedia.org/property/iata> ?iata.} UNION  {?airport <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/iataLocationIdentifier> ?iata. } OPTIONAL { ?airport foaf:homepage ?airport_home. } OPTIONAL { ?airport rdfs:label ?name. } OPTIONAL { ?airport <http://dbpedia.org/property/nativename> ?airport_name.} FILTER ( !bound(?name) || langMatches( lang(?name), 'en') )}
 2.997 PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/> PREFIX geo: <http://www.w3.org/2003/01/geo/wgs84_pos#> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> SELECT * WHERE { {?city rdfs:label 'Ozero'@en.} UNION { ?alias <http://dbpedia.org/property/redirect> ?city;  rdfs:label 'Ozero'@en. } UNION { ?alias <http://dbpedia.org/property/disambiguates> ?city;  rdfs:label 'Ozero'@en. } OPTIONAL { ?city <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/abstract> ?abstract} OPTIONAL { ?city geo:lat ?latitude; geo:long ?longitude}OPTIONAL { ?city foaf:depiction ?image } OPTIONAL { ?city rdfs:label ?name } OPTIONAL { ?city foaf:homepage ?home } OPTIONAL { ?city <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/populationTotal> ?population } OPTIONAL { ?city <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/thumbnail> ?thumbnail } FILTER (langMatches( lang(?abstract), 'en'))}
 66.247 PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> SELECT * WHERE { ?city a <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/Place>; rdfs:label 'Yoactún'@en.  ?airport a <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/Airport>. {?airport <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/city> ?city} UNION {?airport <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/location> ?city} UNION {?airport <http://dbpedia.org/property/cityServed> ?city.} UNION {?airport <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/city> ?city. }{?airport <http://dbpedia.org/property/iata> ?iata.} UNION  {?airport <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/iataLocationIdentifier> ?iata. } OPTIONAL { ?airport foaf:homepage ?airport_home. } OPTIONAL { ?airport rdfs:label ?name. } OPTIONAL { ?airport <http://dbpedia.org/property/nativename> ?airport_name.} FILTER ( !bound(?name) || langMatches( lang(?name), 'pl') )}
 8.582 PREFIX owl: <http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#> PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#> PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/> PREFIX dc: <http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/> PREFIX : <http://dbpedia.org/resource/> PREFIX dbpedia2: <http://dbpedia.org/property/> PREFIX dbpedia: <http://dbpedia.org/> PREFIX skos: <http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#>  				PREFIX dbo: <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/>				 				SELECT ?subject ?name ?population WHERE { 				?subject rdf:type <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/Settlement>. 				?subject dbo:country :Vanuatu . 				?subject rdfs:label ?name . 				FILTER (LANG(?name) = 'en') . 				} 				LIMIT 3000
 2.225 PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX dbpedia: <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/> SELECT ?name ?description ?thumbnail WHERE { 	OPTIONAL { 		<http://dbpedia.org/resource/Zion_Square> rdfs:label ?name FILTER (LANG(?name) = 'en') 	} 	OPTIONAL { 		<http://dbpedia.org/resource/Zion_Square> dbpedia:abstract ?description FILTER (LANG(?description) = 'en') 	} 	OPTIONAL { 		<http://dbpedia.org/resource/Zion_Square> dbpedia:thumbnail ?thumbnail 	} }
 3.887 PREFIX owl: <http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#> PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#> PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/> PREFIX dc: <http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/> PREFIX : <http://dbpedia.org/resource/> PREFIX dbpedia2: <http://dbpedia.org/property/> PREFIX dbpedia: <http://dbpedia.org/> PREFIX skos: <http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#>  				PREFIX dbo: <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/>				 				SELECT ?subject ?name ?population WHERE { 				?subject rdf:type <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/Settlement>. 				?subject dbo:country :Saint_Vincent_and_the_Grenadines . 				?subject rdfs:label ?name . 				FILTER (LANG(?name) = 'en') . 				} 				LIMIT 3000
 34.346 PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#>  PREFIX rdf:<http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#> 	PREFIX dbpedia-owl:<http://dbpedia.org/ontology/> 	PREFIX dbpedia:<http://dbpedia.org/resource/> 	PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/>  	select ?lien ?label ?perso ?nom where {dbpedia:Eric_Tsang ?lien ?perso. ?perso rdf:type dbpedia-owl:Person. ?perso foaf:name ?nom. ?lien rdfs:label ?label}
